SELECT [p0].[ProductID], [p0].[Brand], [p0].[CategoryId], [p0].[CreatedAt], [p0].[CreatedById], [p0].[Description], [p0].[GalleryImages], [p0].[IsAvailable], [p0].[IsDeleted], [p0].[IsFeatured], [p0].[IsNewProduct], [p0].[IsPublished], [p0].[MainImage], [p0].[ModifiedById], [p0].[Name], [p0].[Price], [p0].[Slug], [p0].[Specifications], [p0].[StockQuantity], [p0].[UpdatedAt], [c].[CategoryID], [c].[CreatedAt], [c].[CreatedById], [c].[Description], [c].[ImageUrl], [c].[IsDeleted], [c].[ModifiedById], [c].[Name], [c].[Slug], [c].[UpdatedAt]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(@p) [p].[ProductID], [p].[Brand], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[CreatedById], [p].[Description], [p].[GalleryImages], [p].[IsAvailable], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFeatured], [p].[IsNewProduct], [p].[IsPublished], [p].[MainImage], [p].[ModifiedById], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[Slug], [p].[Specifications], [p].[StockQuantity], [p].[UpdatedAt]

SELECT [c].[CartID], [c].[CreatedAt], [c].[CreatedById], [c].[IsActive], [c].[IsDeleted], [c].[LastAbandonedCartEmailSentAt], [c].[ModifiedById], [c].[SessionId], [c].[UpdatedAt], [c].[UserId], [u].[Id], [s].[CartItemID], [s].[CartId], [s].[CreatedAt], [s].[CreatedById], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[ModifiedById], [s].[ProductId], [s].[Quantity], [s].[UnitPrice], [s].[UpdatedAt], [s].[ProductID0], [s].[Brand], [s].[CategoryId], [s].[CreatedAt0], [s].[CreatedById0], [s].[Description], [s].[GalleryImages], [s].[IsAvailable], [s].[IsDeleted0], [s].[IsFeatured], [s].[IsNewProduct], [s].[IsPublished], [s].[MainImage], [s].[ModifiedById0], [s].[Name], [s].[Price], [s].[Slug], [s].[Specifications], [s].[StockQuantity], [s].[UpdatedAt0], [u].[AccessFailedCount], [u].[ConcurrencyStamp], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[CreatedById], [u].[Email], [u].[EmailConfirmed], [u].[FirstName], [u].[IsActive], [u].[IsDeleted], [u].[LastName], [u].[LockoutEnabled], [u].[LockoutEnd], [u].[ModifiedById], [u].[NormalizedEmail], [u].[NormalizedUserName], [u].[PasswordHash], [u].[PhoneNumber], [u].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [u].[RegistrationDate], [u].[SecurityStamp], [u].[TwoFactorEnabled], [u].[UpdatedAt], [u].[UserName]
FROM [Carts] AS [c]
LEFT JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [c].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c1].[CartItemID], [c1].[CartId], [c1].[CreatedAt], [c1].[CreatedById], [c1].[IsDeleted], [c1].[ModifiedById], [c1].[ProductId], [c1].[Quantity], [c1].[UnitPrice], [c1].[UpdatedAt], [p0].[ProductID] AS [ProductID0], [p0].[Brand], [p0].[CategoryId], [p0].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt0], [p0].[CreatedById] AS [CreatedById0], [p0].[Description], [p0].[GalleryImages], [p0].[IsAvailable], [p0].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted0], [p0].[IsFeatured], [p0].[IsNewProduct], [p0].[IsPublished], [p0].[MainImage], [p0].[ModifiedById] AS [ModifiedById0], [p0].[Name], [p0].[Price], [p0].[Slug], [p0].[Specifications], [p0].[StockQuantity], [p0].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt0]
    FROM [CartItems] AS [c1]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [p].[ProductID], [p].[Brand], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[CreatedById], [p].[Description], [p].[GalleryImages], [p].[IsAvailable], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFeatured], [p].[IsNewProduct], [p].[IsPublished], [p].[MainImage], [p].[ModifiedById], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[Slug], [p].[Specifications], [p].[StockQuantity], [p].[UpdatedAt]
        FROM [Products] AS [p]
        WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ) AS [p0] ON [c1].[ProductId] = [p0].[ProductID]
    WHERE [c1].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s] ON [c].[CartID] = [s].[CartId]
WHERE [c].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [c].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit) AND [c].[UserId] IS NOT NULL AND EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM [CartItems] AS [c0]

SELECT [c].[CartID], [c].[CreatedAt], [c].[CreatedById], [c].[IsActive], [c].[IsDeleted], [c].[LastAbandonedCartEmailSentAt], [c].[ModifiedById], [c].[SessionId], [c].[UpdatedAt], [c].[UserId], [u].[Id], [s].[CartItemID], [s].[CartId], [s].[CreatedAt], [s].[CreatedById], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[ModifiedById], [s].[ProductId], [s].[Quantity], [s].[UnitPrice], [s].[UpdatedAt], [s].[ProductID0], [s].[Brand], [s].[CategoryId], [s].[CreatedAt0], [s].[CreatedById0], [s].[Description], [s].[GalleryImages], [s].[IsAvailable], [s].[IsDeleted0], [s].[IsFeatured], [s].[IsNewProduct], [s].[IsPublished], [s].[MainImage], [s].[ModifiedById0], [s].[Name], [s].[Price], [s].[Slug], [s].[Specifications], [s].[StockQuantity], [s].[UpdatedAt0], [u].[AccessFailedCount], [u].[ConcurrencyStamp], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[CreatedById], [u].[Email], [u].[EmailConfirmed], [u].[FirstName], [u].[IsActive], [u].[IsDeleted], [u].[LastName], [u].[LockoutEnabled], [u].[LockoutEnd], [u].[ModifiedById], [u].[NormalizedEmail], [u].[NormalizedUserName], [u].[PasswordHash], [u].[PhoneNumber], [u].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [u].[RegistrationDate], [u].[SecurityStamp], [u].[TwoFactorEnabled], [u].[UpdatedAt], [u].[UserName]
FROM [Carts] AS [c]
LEFT JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [c].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c1].[CartItemID], [c1].[CartId], [c1].[CreatedAt], [c1].[CreatedById], [c1].[IsDeleted], [c1].[ModifiedById], [c1].[ProductId], [c1].[Quantity], [c1].[UnitPrice], [c1].[UpdatedAt], [p0].[ProductID] AS [ProductID0], [p0].[Brand], [p0].[CategoryId], [p0].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt0], [p0].[CreatedById] AS [CreatedById0], [p0].[Description], [p0].[GalleryImages], [p0].[IsAvailable], [p0].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted0], [p0].[IsFeatured], [p0].[IsNewProduct], [p0].[IsPublished], [p0].[MainImage], [p0].[ModifiedById] AS [ModifiedById0], [p0].[Name], [p0].[Price], [p0].[Slug], [p0].[Specifications], [p0].[StockQuantity], [p0].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt0]
    FROM [CartItems] AS [c1]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [p].[ProductID], [p].[Brand], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[CreatedById], [p].[Description], [p].[GalleryImages], [p].[IsAvailable], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFeatured], [p].[IsNewProduct], [p].[IsPublished], [p].[MainImage], [p].[ModifiedById], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[Slug], [p].[Specifications], [p].[StockQuantity], [p].[UpdatedAt]
        FROM [Products] AS [p]
        WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ) AS [p0] ON [c1].[ProductId] = [p0].[ProductID]
    WHERE [c1].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s] ON [c].[CartID] = [s].[CartId]
WHERE [c].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [c].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit) AND [c].[UserId] IS NOT NULL AND EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM [CartItems] AS [c0]
    WHERE [c0].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [c].[CartID] = [c0].[CartId]) AND COALESCE([c].[UpdatedAt], [c].[CreatedAt]) < @updatedBefore AND ([c].[LastAbandonedCartEmailSentAt] IS NULL OR [c].[LastAbandonedCartEmailSentAt] < @emailCooldownBefore)

LEFT JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [c].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c1].[CartItemID], [c1].[CartId], [c1].[CreatedAt], [c1].[CreatedById], [c1].[IsDeleted], [c1].[ModifiedById], [c1].[ProductId], [c1].[Quantity], [c1].[UnitPrice], [c1].[UpdatedAt], [p0].[ProductID] AS [ProductID0], [p0].[Brand], [p0].[CategoryId], [p0].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt0], [p0].[CreatedById] AS [CreatedById0], [p0].[Description], [p0].[GalleryImages], [p0].[IsAvailable], [p0].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted0], [p0].[IsFeatured], [p0].[IsNewProduct], [p0].[IsPublished], [p0].[MainImage], [p0].[ModifiedById] AS [ModifiedById0], [p0].[Name], [p0].[Price], [p0].[Slug], [p0].[Specifications], [p0].[StockQuantity], [p0].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt0]

        SELECT [p].[ProductID], [p].[Brand], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[CreatedById], [p].[Description], [p].[GalleryImages], [p].[IsAvailable], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFeatured], [p].[IsNewProduct], [p].[IsPublished], [p].[MainImage], [p].[ModifiedById], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[Slug], [p].[Specifications], [p].[StockQuantity], [p].[UpdatedAt]

        WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ) AS [p0] ON [c1].[ProductId] = [p0].[ProductID]

) AS [s] ON [c].[CartID] = [s].[CartId]

FROM [Carts] AS [c]
LEFT JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [c].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c1].[CartItemID], [c1].[CartId], [c1].[CreatedAt], [c1].[CreatedById], [c1].[IsDeleted], [c1].[ModifiedById], [c1].[ProductId], [c1].[Quantity], [c1].[UnitPrice], [c1].[UpdatedAt], [p0].[ProductID] AS [ProductID0], [p0].[Brand], [p0].[CategoryId], [p0].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt0], [p0].[CreatedById] AS [CreatedById0], [p0].[Description], [p0].[GalleryImages], [p0].[IsAvailable], [p0].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted0], [p0].[IsFeatured], [p0].[IsNewProduct], [p0].[IsPublished], [p0].[MainImage], [p0].[ModifiedById] AS [ModifiedById0], [p0].[Name], [p0].[Price], [p0].[Slug], [p0].[Specifications], [p0].[StockQuantity], [p0].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt0]
    FROM [CartItems] AS [c1]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [p].[ProductID], [p].[Brand], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[CreatedById], [p].[Description], [p].[GalleryImages], [p].[IsAvailable], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFeatured], [p].[IsNewProduct], [p].[IsPublished], [p].[MainImage], [p].[ModifiedById], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[Slug], [p].[Specifications], [p].[StockQuantity], [p].[UpdatedAt]

        WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ) AS [p0] ON [c1].[ProductId] = [p0].[ProductID]
    WHERE [c1].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s] ON [c].[CartID] = [s].[CartId]

    FROM [CartItems] AS [c0]

SELECT [c].[CartID], [c].[CreatedAt], [c].[CreatedById], [c].[IsActive], [c].[IsDeleted], [c].[LastAbandonedCartEmailSentAt], [c].[ModifiedById], [c].[SessionId], [c].[UpdatedAt], [c].[UserId], [u].[Id], [s].[CartItemID], [s].[CartId], [s].[CreatedAt], [s].[CreatedById], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[ModifiedById], [s].[ProductId], [s].[Quantity], [s].[UnitPrice], [s].[UpdatedAt], [s].[ProductID0], [s].[Brand], [s].[CategoryId], [s].[CreatedAt0], [s].[CreatedById0], [s].[Description], [s].[GalleryImages], [s].[IsAvailable], [s].[IsDeleted0], [s].[IsFeatured], [s].[IsNewProduct], [s].[IsPublished], [s].[MainImage], [s].[ModifiedById0], [s].[Name], [s].[Price], [s].[Slug], [s].[Specifications], [s].[StockQuantity], [s].[UpdatedAt0], [u].[AccessFailedCount], [u].[ConcurrencyStamp], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[CreatedById], [u].[Email], [u].[EmailConfirmed], [u].[FirstName], [u].[IsActive], [u].[IsDeleted], [u].[LastName], [u].[LockoutEnabled], [u].[LockoutEnd], [u].[ModifiedById], [u].[NormalizedEmail], [u].[NormalizedUserName], [u].[PasswordHash], [u].[PhoneNumber], [u].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [u].[RegistrationDate], [u].[SecurityStamp], [u].[TwoFactorEnabled], [u].[UpdatedAt], [u].[UserName]
FROM [Carts] AS [c]
LEFT JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [c].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c1].[CartItemID], [c1].[CartId], [c1].[CreatedAt], [c1].[CreatedById], [c1].[IsDeleted], [c1].[ModifiedById], [c1].[ProductId], [c1].[Quantity], [c1].[UnitPrice], [c1].[UpdatedAt], [p0].[ProductID] AS [ProductID0], [p0].[Brand], [p0].[CategoryId], [p0].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt0], [p0].[CreatedById] AS [CreatedById0], [p0].[Description], [p0].[GalleryImages], [p0].[IsAvailable], [p0].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted0], [p0].[IsFeatured], [p0].[IsNewProduct], [p0].[IsPublished], [p0].[MainImage], [p0].[ModifiedById] AS [ModifiedById0], [p0].[Name], [p0].[Price], [p0].[Slug], [p0].[Specifications], [p0].[StockQuantity], [p0].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt0]
    FROM [CartItems] AS [c1]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [p].[ProductID], [p].[Brand], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[CreatedById], [p].[Description], [p].[GalleryImages], [p].[IsAvailable], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFeatured], [p].[IsNewProduct], [p].[IsPublished], [p].[MainImage], [p].[ModifiedById], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[Slug], [p].[Specifications], [p].[StockQuantity], [p].[UpdatedAt]
        FROM [Products] AS [p]
        WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ) AS [p0] ON [c1].[ProductId] = [p0].[ProductID]
    WHERE [c1].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s] ON [c].[CartID] = [s].[CartId]
WHERE [c].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [c].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit) AND [c].[UserId] IS NOT NULL AND EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM [CartItems] AS [c0]
    WHERE [c0].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [c].[CartID] = [c0].[CartId]) AND COALESCE([c].[UpdatedAt], [c].[CreatedAt]) < @updatedBefore AND ([c].[LastAbandonedCartEmailSentAt] IS NULL OR [c].[LastAbandonedCartEmailSentAt] < @emailCooldownBefore)

SELECT [c].[CartID], [c].[CreatedAt], [c].[CreatedById], [c].[IsActive], [c].[IsDeleted], [c].[LastAbandonedCartEmailSentAt], [c].[ModifiedById], [c].[SessionId], [c].[UpdatedAt], [c].[UserId], [u].[Id], [s].[CartItemID], [s].[CartId], [s].[CreatedAt], [s].[CreatedById], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[ModifiedById], [s].[ProductId], [s].[Quantity], [s].[UnitPrice], [s].[UpdatedAt], [s].[ProductID0], [s].[Brand], [s].[CategoryId], [s].[CreatedAt0], [s].[CreatedById0], [s].[Description], [s].[GalleryImages], [s].[IsAvailable], [s].[IsDeleted0], [s].[IsFeatured], [s].[IsNewProduct], [s].[IsPublished], [s].[MainImage], [s].[ModifiedById0], [s].[Name], [s].[Price], [s].[Slug], [s].[Specifications], [s].[StockQuantity], [s].[UpdatedAt0], [u].[AccessFailedCount], [u].[ConcurrencyStamp], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[CreatedById], [u].[Email], [u].[EmailConfirmed], [u].[FirstName], [u].[IsActive], [u].[IsDeleted], [u].[LastName], [u].[LockoutEnabled], [u].[LockoutEnd], [u].[ModifiedById], [u].[NormalizedEmail], [u].[NormalizedUserName], [u].[PasswordHash], [u].[PhoneNumber], [u].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [u].[RegistrationDate], [u].[SecurityStamp], [u].[TwoFactorEnabled], [u].[UpdatedAt], [u].[UserName]
FROM [Carts] AS [c]
LEFT JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [c].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c1].[CartItemID], [c1].[CartId], [c1].[CreatedAt], [c1].[CreatedById], [c1].[IsDeleted], [c1].[ModifiedById], [c1].[ProductId], [c1].[Quantity], [c1].[UnitPrice], [c1].[UpdatedAt], [p0].[ProductID] AS [ProductID0], [p0].[Brand], [p0].[CategoryId], [p0].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt0], [p0].[CreatedById] AS [CreatedById0], [p0].[Description], [p0].[GalleryImages], [p0].[IsAvailable], [p0].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted0], [p0].[IsFeatured], [p0].[IsNewProduct], [p0].[IsPublished], [p0].[MainImage], [p0].[ModifiedById] AS [ModifiedById0], [p0].[Name], [p0].[Price], [p0].[Slug], [p0].[Specifications], [p0].[StockQuantity], [p0].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt0]
    FROM [CartItems] AS [c1]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [p].[ProductID], [p].[Brand], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[CreatedById], [p].[Description], [p].[GalleryImages], [p].[IsAvailable], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFeatured], [p].[IsNewProduct], [p].[IsPublished], [p].[MainImage], [p].[ModifiedById], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[Slug], [p].[Specifications], [p].[StockQuantity], [p].[UpdatedAt]
        FROM [Products] AS [p]
        WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ) AS [p0] ON [c1].[ProductId] = [p0].[ProductID]
    WHERE [c1].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [s] ON [c].[CartID] = [s].[CartId]
WHERE [c].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [c].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit) AND [c].[UserId] IS NOT NULL AND EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM [CartItems] AS [c0]
